## Chapter 9 {.heading_98-0}

9:1 Now in the twelfth month, that is, the month Adar, on the thirteenth day of the same, when the king's commandment and his decree drew near to be put in execution, in the day that the enemies of the Jews hoped to have power over them, (though it was turned to the contrary, that the Jews had rule over them that hated them;)

2 The Jews gathered themselves together in their cities throughout all the provinces of the king Ahasuerus, to lay hand on such as sought their hurt: and no man could withstand them; for the fear of them fell upon all people.

3 And all the rulers of the provinces, and the lieutenants, and the deputies, and officers of the king, helped the Jews; because the fear of Mordecai fell upon them.

4 For Mordecai was great in the king's house, and his fame went out throughout all the provinces: for this man Mordecai waxed greater and greater.

["The twelfth month" ]{.class_3428}of verse 1 would correspond to our February--March lunar month. All the chronologists give the date for the events of verse 1 as March 7, 473 B.C.

Now, there is something in verse 1 which has to do with the Second Advent, but nobody has it figured out yet. The Advent itself takes place in September-October at the Feast of Tabernacles (see comments on Neh. 8:13--17 and Matt. 17:1--5 in those commentaries). There could a five-month interval between the Advent proper and the beginning of the Millennial reign. Unfortunately until the Lord shows somebody more than has been revealed through Larkin, Scofield, Pentecost, Gaebelein, Bullinger, Ruckman, and all the other prophecy teachers, there are no real answers for the [time discrepancies ]{.class_3429}that accompany the end of the Tribulation, the Second Advent, and the beginning of the Millennium.

There are variations of numbers at the end of the Tribulation that nobody has yet figured out. There is the [cleansing of the sanctuary]{.class_3429} (Dan. 8:14). There are also two other [undefined time periods]{.class_3429} measured from the middle of the Tribulation when the daily sacrifice is taken away and ["the abomination that maketh desolate"]{.class_3428} is set up (Dan. 12:11--12).

Twice in the Olivet discourse, Christ warns about the time of the Tribulation being [shortened ]{.class_3429}(Matt. 24:22, 48--51). There is a variation in time at the end of the Tribulation that no one yet understands.

Now, the moment of truth arrived for the Jews. Two immutable decrees were on the law books. The first decree was made by a man who made the decree without the full knowledge of the king as to the details of the law. That man now hangs dead on a 75-foot gallows. Moreover, the first decree sets all of its supporters against the queen who has twice come unbidden to the king and has received his acceptance both times.

The second decree has been made with the king's full approval. It was made by the queen's cousin who now manages all the wealth and property of the man hanging on the gallows. The cousin of the queen has favor of the king because he saved his life. He now is not only arrayed as a king, but he has the full authority of the king upon his hand---[the king's signet ring.]{.class_3429}

The first decree is "Kill the Jews and you will be paid." The second decree is "The king supports the Jews defending themselves." Every member of the Persian Empire had to choose which decree he would follow.

Given the facts listed above, a man would be a fool to see how much he could get away with by following the first decree. You would be better off remaining neutral in the fight, rather than siding against the king and his chief lawmaker. After all, the fellow who made that first decree is no longer around to help you.

All the rulers in the kingdom saw the problem immediately. They may have had no love for the Jews (Ezra 5), but they figured ["a living dog]{.class_3428} \[Mordecai in this instance\] [is better than a dead lion ]{.class_3428}\[Haman\][" ]{.class_3428}(Eccl. 9:4). [Mordecai ]{.class_3429}was alive and could enact retribution on anyone who might manage to get the upper hand on some Jew. So out of ["fear of Mordecai" ]{.class_3428}[]{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_403}all of the minor officials in the empire ["helped the Jews" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 3).

Verse 4:[ "For Mordecai was great in the king's house, and his fame went out throughout all the provinces: for this man Mordecai waxed greater and greater." ]{.class_3428}Mordecai becomes one of three Jews to rule alongside a Gentile king in his kingdom. [Joseph ]{.class_3429}is the prime minister of Pharaoh back in Genesis, and [Daniel ]{.class_3429}is made the first of three presidents under Darius the Mede in the Persian Empire (Dan. 6). In the Bible, whenever a Gentile nation put a Jew in a high position of leadership, that nation went right to the top politically and economically.

Back in the nineteenth century, [Benjamin Disraeli]{.class_3429} served as Prime Minister to Queen Victoria in England; he was a Jew. [During that time, Britain reached the heights of her empire.]{.class_3429}

America has never had a Jewish president or vice-president (although Hitler often accused Roosevelt of being a Jew). The closest we have ever come was when Al Gore made Senator Joseph Lieberman his running mate in the 2000 election, and Lieberman was a liberal Democrat from Massachusetts who believed in abortion, homosexual marriages, no prayer or Bible reading in public schools, and the entire secular agenda.

But America has distinguished itself among the Gentile nations of the world in that it is one of only [two nations]{.class_3429} that have never nationally persecuted that Jew (Holland being the other nation).

The president of the Jewish congregation of Newport, Rhode Island, in a letter to President Washington in 1790, said of the newly formed United States of America: "which to bigotry gives no sanction, to persecution no assistance" (quote taken from the Jewish-American Hall of Fame website, 2000).

This country reached the height of its power in World War II when America was responsible for delivering those Jews in Europe from Hitler's concentration camps. And if it hadn't been for the support of a cussing Baptist (Harry Truman), [Israel wouldn't have been granted its status as a nation in 1948.]{.class_3429}

The problems America has started back in the 1930s when Prohibition was repealed and the nation voted to be a country of drunks. From that time to this God has never again sent a national []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_404}revival. We have been on a downhill slide morally ever since. The Supreme Court threw prayer and the Bible out of the schools because they were against the "establishment clause" of the First Amendment to the Bill of Rights and then declared [pornography ]{.class_3429}and [abortion ]{.class_3429}as Constitutionally protected rights. So drug use, fornication, and the VD rate sky-rocketed; kids began to kill their teachers and other kids in the public schools; and the faggots and queers came "out of the closet" and began to recruit your kids into their perversion.

[Morally ]{.class_3429}America is shot and awaiting the judgment of God. The only thing we have left is that we have been [a friend to Israel,]{.class_3429} and the Lord blesses those [nations that have blessed His people]{.class_3429} (Gen. 12:1--3; Num. 24:9).

Meanwhile the government (the President, the Supreme Court, and both houses of Congress) has steadily surrendered our national sovereignty to the United Nations. We can't even blow our nose overseas without asking the UN's permission first.

As a body, the United Nations has been [anti-Israel]{.class_3429} since its inception. Every time Israel tries to defend herself, the UN steps in to protect the Arabs from losing land from which they can launch their next attack against the Jewish State (see [Israel: A Deadly Piece of Dirt]{.class_3429}, Bible Baptist Bookstore, 2001).

So here is America. We're torn between our long standing relationship to the Jews because of our country's Biblical heritage and our subservience to the UN which wants the Jews out of Israel and a "Palestinian" State in its place. So far all we have done is talk, compromise, and sit back and do nothing to stop Arafat and the PLO (now called the PA---the Palestinian "Authority") [from bombing Israelis in their own country. ]{.class_3429}We haven't yet taken an active role against Israel. We are still the closest thing to a friend that Israel has.

Just let that status [change]{.class_3429}, and you will see the Lord let all "hell" brake loose in this country. "9--11" won't be anything to what will come when this country actually lifts a hand against Israel. Eventually (Zeph. 3:8; Jer. 30:11), it will happen.

9:5 Thus the Jews smote all their enemies with the stroke of the sword, and slaughter, and destruction, and []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_405}did what they would unto those that hated them.

6 And in Shushan the palace the Jews slew and destroyed five hundred men.

7 And Parshandatha, and Dalphon, and Aspatha,

8 And Poratha, and Adalia, and Aridatha,

9 And Parmashta, and Arisai, and Aridai, and Vajezatha,

10 The ten sons of Haman the son of Hammedatha, the enemy of the Jews, slew they; but on the spoil laid they not their hand.

11 On that day the number of those that were slain in Shushan the palace was brought before the king.

You would think that with the king himself against them, that the enemies of the Jews would have gone underground rather than try to enforce Haman's decree. But between the time Haman was hung and ["the thirteenth day"]{.class_3428} of ["the month Adar,"]{.class_3428} there were ten sons of Haman who were stirring up a bunch of folks to go ahead and attack the Jews. Those ten sons are given by name in verses 7--9. They managed to convince at least 800 people in Shushan itself (vss. 6 and 15) and 75,000 others in the rest of the provinces (vs. 16).

Of course with such odds stacked against them, it is obvious that these people were driven by an unreasoning hatred of the Jews that had completely blinded their good judgment. As I said in my comments under Esther 3:5, that unreasoning hatred of the Jews is a Satanic thing. The Devil hates the Jewish people because they brought forth[ the Messiah]{.class_3429}, and the Messiah was his undoing. [His hatred against the Jewish race endures forever.]{.class_3429}

In the book of Esther, the hatred of Satan against the Jews is symbolized by[ one man. ]{.class_3429}Six times in the book Haman is referred to as the Jews' enemy (Esth. 3:10, 7:4,6, 8:1, 9:10, 9:24). In this chapter he is called ["the enemy of the Jews" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 10) and ["the enemy of all the Jews" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 24).

Now the lesson here is, don't be anti-Jewish. That doesn't mean that you have to agree with everything that every Jew does. They're still sinners just like everyone else, see. But don't start blaming them as a people for everything that goes wrong. When you start doing that you are as much in the realm of the Devil as if you went and []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_406}joined the Church of Satan.

9:12 And the king said unto Esther the queen, The Jews have slain and destroyed five hundred men in Shushan the palace, and the ten sons of Haman; what have they done in the rest of the king's provinces? now what is thy petition? and it shall be granted thee: or what is thy request further? and it shall be done.

13 Then said Esther, If it please the king, let it be granted to the Jews which are in Shushan to do to morrow also according unto this day's decree, and let Haman's ten sons be hanged upon the gallows.

14 And the king commanded it so to be done: and the decree was given at Shushan; and they hanged Haman's ten sons.

15 For the Jews that were in Shushan gathered themselves together on the fourteenth day also of the month Adar, and slew three hundred men at Shushan; but on the prey they laid not their hand.

16 But the other Jews that were in the king's provinces gathered themselves together, and stood for their lives, and had rest from their enemies, and slew of their foes seventy and five thousand, but they laid not their hands on the prey,

["The thirteenth day"]{.class_3428} of Adar has now come and gone in this passage. At the end of the day, the Jews have killed 500 of their enemies and ["Haman's]{.class_3428} [ten sons."]{.class_3428} According to Haman's law, that day was the only "legal" day for the Gentiles to attack and kill the Jews. But there are still a bunch of people in Shushan who are more concerned about the "spirit" of the law (the destruction of the Jews) than they are the "letter" of the law. There are at least 300 men who have a plot to kill Jews the next day when no one is suspecting it.

Evidently, Esther has discovered this plot, for she asks the king to grant the Jews [one more day of protection. ]{.class_3429}As a sign to those who are planning the attack, she has ["the ten sons of Haman" ]{.class_3428}that were killed hung on the same gallows on which their father was hung.

That was a common practice in the ancient and medieval world. []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_407}A conquering king would hang the dead bodies of his victims up in a public place to let everyone know what would happen to anyone that opposed him. Sometimes they would cut off the heads and stick them on stakes.

The Assyrians used to leave hills of the skulls of those they had conquered outside any city they took. When the Romans destroyed Jerusalem in A.D. 70, [they crucified 500 Jews along the roads leading to Jerusalem. ]{.class_3429}Joshua hung up the five Canaanite kings who fought against him in Joshua 10.

The one ruler in history most famous for hanging his victims in public for display was Vlad Tepes of Transylvania, the real man behind the legend of Dracula. He was known as "Vlad the Impaler" because he loved to impale his enemies on stakes and watch them die. At one time he had over 20,000 impaled bodies of the Turks outside of the city where he ruled.

You have to admit those kinds of things would shake you up and make you think twice before you tried anything with a ruler or army like that. It was an early form of "psychological" warfare.

[Prophetically, ]{.class_3429}in the passage before us, you have a man who is called ["the enemy of the Jews." ]{.class_3428}He is one of the greatest types of Satan and the Antichrist in the Bible. He has [ten sons]{.class_3429} who try to help him in the destruction of the Jews. You will recall that, in the book of Revelation, both the dragon (Rev. 12:3) and the beast (Rev. 13:1) have ["ten horns." ]{.class_3428}Those ["ten horns" ]{.class_3428}represent ["ten kings"]{.class_3428} who rule with the Antichrist.

Verse 16 gives the total number of Gentiles slain by the Jews throughout the empire. According to rabbinical tradition, of the 75,000 that were slain, 70,000 were Amalekites. Of course, there is no way of knowing if that were true or not.

9:17 On the thirteenth day of the month Adar; and on the fourteenth day of the same rested they, and made it a day of feasting and gladness.

18 But the Jews that were at Shushan assembled together on the thirteenth day thereof, and on the fourteenth thereof; and on the fifteenth day of the same they rested, and made it a day of feasting and gladness.

19 Therefore the Jews of the villages, that dwelt in the unwalled towns, made the fourteenth day of the month Adar a day of gladness and feasting, and a good day, and of sending portions one to another.

20 And Mordecai wrote these things, and sent letters unto all the Jews that were in all the provinces of the king Ahasuerus, both nigh and far,

21 To stablish this among them, that they should keep the fourteenth day of the month Adar, and the fifteenth day of the same, yearly,

22 As the days wherein the Jews rested from their enemies, and the month which was turned unto them from sorrow to joy, and from mourning into a good day: that they should make them days of feasting and joy, and of sending portions one to another, and gifts to the poor.

23 And the Jews undertook to do as they had begun, and as Mordecai had written unto them;

24 Because Haman the son of Hammedatha, the Agagite, the enemy of all the Jews, had devised against the Jews to destroy them, and had cast Pur, that is, the lot, to consume them, and to destroy them;

25 But when Esther came before the king, he commanded by letters that his wicked device, which he devised against the Jews, should return upon his own head, and that he and his sons should be hanged on the gallows.

26 Wherefore they called these days Purim after the name of Pur. Therefore for all the words of this letter, and of that which they had seen concerning this matter, and which had come unto them,

27 The Jews ordained, and took upon them, and upon their seed, and upon all such as joined themselves unto them, so as it should not fail, that they would keep these two days according to their writing, and according to their appointed time every year;

28 And that these days should be remembered and kept throughout every generation, every family, every []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_409}province, and every city; and that these days of Purim should not fail from among the Jews, nor the memorial of them perish from their seed.

29 Then Esther the queen, the daughter of Abihail, and Mordecai the Jew, wrote with all authority, to confirm this second letter of Purim.

30 And he sent the letters unto all the Jews, to the hundred twenty and seven provinces of the kingdom of Ahasuerus, with words of peace and truth,

31 To confirm these days of Purim in their times appointed, according as Mordecai the Jew and Esther the queen had enjoined them, and as they had decreed for themselves and for their seed, the matters of the fastings and their cry.

32 And the decree of Esther confirmed these matters of Purim; and it was written in the book.

This passage describes the establishment of a new Jewish feast day. In the Law, the Lord only gave [seven ]{.class_3429}(Lev. 23), and each of these has prophetic significance. [The Passover]{.class_3429} foreshadows the sacrifice of Christ on the cross (1 Cor. 5:7). The [Feast of Unleavened Bread,]{.class_3429} which followed the Passover, is a picture of Christ's sinlessness. The next feast, the [Feast of the Firstfruits,]{.class_3429} points to the resurrection of Jesus Christ (1 Cor. 15:23). Of course, the [Feast of Pentecost]{.class_3429} is associated with the Body of Christ (Acts 2). Notice that it is on the first day of the week (Lev. 23:16) when Christians meet (John 20:19--26) and that the bread of Pentecost was made with leaven (Lev. 23:17) because the Body of Christ is made up of saved [sinners]{.class_3429}.

The next of the seven feasts is the [Feast of Trumpets. ]{.class_3429}While some expositors try to make this feast prophecy the Rapture of the Church, notice that there is a definite break between the Feast of Pentecost and the Feast of Trumpets, in Leviticus 23:23--24. The Lord makes a definite point of beginning His discussion of the feasts of the seventh month by saying, ["Speak unto THE CHILDREN OF ISRAEL, saying\...." ]{.class_3428}The Feast of Trumpets is the post-Tribulation rapture of Jewish saints (see [The Two Raptures]{.class_3429}, Bible Baptist Bookstore, 1996). The [Day of Atonement]{.class_3429}[]{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_410} is fulfilled when Acts 3:19--21 takes place at the Second Advent. The final and most important of the feasts, the [Feast of Tabernacles,]{.class_3429} is associated with the Millennial reign of Christ (see comments under Neh. 8:14--18).

Now, those are the feasts that were actually instituted by the Lord. In addition, the Jews have [two more feasts]{.class_3442} they celebrate. One of them is the [Feast of Lights,]{.class_3442} [Hanukkah]{.class_3442}. It is not a Biblical feast at all; that is, it is not a feast found anywhere in the Old Testament. It is mentioned in the New Testament in John 10:22 where it is called[ "the feast of the dedication."]{.class_3428}

It is called that because during the 400 years between the Old and the New Testaments, a Syrian tyrant named Antiochas Epiphanes defiled the temple by slaughtering a pig on the altar and spraying its blood all over the temple walls. A family of priests (the Maccabees) revolted against the Syrians and eventually overthrew them. After the war, the temple was cleansed. Supposedly there was only enough oil to keep the golden candlesticks, which were to be burning continually, lit for one day. According to tradition, God kept the lamps lit for eight days until new oil arrived to replenish the candlesticks. 

That story isn't recorded in the Bible. It is recorded in the Apocryphal book of [I Maccabees]{.class_3429}, which is the most historical of all the Apocryphal literature. It is [not ]{.class_3429}inspired Scripture; it is a mixture of history, tradition, and little bit of pagan superstition.

Although the Lord did honor the feast by attending it, it is a rather minor feast, spiritually speaking. It has received a lot of attention because of its proximity to Christmas. But all that is about is \$\$\$; it has nothing to do with the Bible, salvation (in any Biblical sense of the word), or God.

The other feast observed by the Jews is found here in Esther 9. It is called the [Feast of Purim;]{.class_3429} i.e., the [Feast of Lots. ]{.class_3429}It is named after the fact that Haman cast lots to decide the day the Jews would be killed (vs.26 cf. Esth. 3:7).

You will notice that at first the celebration was completely spontaneous: verses 17--18. The Jews outside of the capitol celebrated ["on the fourteenth"]{.class_3428} of Adar, the day after they slaughtered the Gentiles who attacked them. But because the Jews of Shushan had to fight two days, they celebrated []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_411}["on the fifteenth day"]{.class_3428} (vs.18).

Before the holiday was ever named or universally observed, ["the Jews of the villages, that dwelt in the unwalled towns, made the fourteenth day of the month Adar a day of gladness and feasting, and a good day, and of sending portions one to another" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 19). The verse is similar to Nehemiah 8:10 where the ["good day" ]{.class_3428}is called a ["day holy unto our Lord."]{.class_3428}

And although the circumstances of Esther 9 are different than Nehemiah 8, the [sentiment ]{.class_3429}is still the same. The idea is that God delivered them and made it possible to freely serve Him. Therefore, they were setting a special day apart in remembrance for what God had done for them. That was the reason behind [Passover ]{.class_3429}and the [Feast of Unleavened Bread]{.class_3429} (Exod. 13). It was to celebrate the Jews' deliverance from Egypt by the hand of God.

In fact, the word [holiday]{.class_3429} is actually a contraction of "holy" and "day." The original meaning of the word is "a day set apart for God." The celebration was to observe some special act of God.

The [four ]{.class_3429}original holidays in America were [Christmas, Easter, Independence Day, and Thanksgiving Day. ]{.class_3429}Each of those had something to do with God: the birth of His Son, the resurrection of His Son, His Providential care in the creation of this nation, and His goodness toward the people of this country.

Today we have so many "holidays" (observed and unobserved) that they have lost all connection to anything God has done. What does Labor Day or Martin Luther King Jr. Day have to do with anything God has done for this country, I ask you? [Not one cotton-pickin' thing on this earth, man! ]{.class_3429}Each is just one more day to try to exploit for a buck.

In this passage the Jews are remembering how God used Esther and Mordecai to save them from genocide at the hands of Haman and his sons.

Mordecai makes both days, the fourteenth and the fifteenth, days of celebration to be universally observed by the Jews (vss. 20--22). The letter Mordecai sends out is called the ["second letter of Purim"]{.class_3428} in verse 29. The first letter was the decree passed by []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_412}Mordecai with the king's ring back in Esther 8:9--13. Unlike the first letter, this second decree by Mordecai was to the Jews alone, not to everyone in the kingdom. Nevertheless, the letter still carried the full authority of the king (vs. 29).

Verse 28 says, ["And that these days should be remembered and kept throughout every generation\...and that these days of Purim should not fail from among the Jews, nor the memorial of them perish from their seed." ]{.class_3428}And of course the Feast of Purim is observed by all Jews throughout the world to this day. It falls sometime on our calendar in the last half of [February ]{.class_3429}or the beginning of [March]{.class_3429}.

In some ways, Purim has degenerated to a children's holiday like Halloween, but without the Satanic or demonic overtones. The kids all dress up in costumes and go to parties and carnivals. In accordance with Mordecai's command ["of sending portions one to another, and gifts to the poor" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 22), the Jews will usually give sweets and pastries to their acquaintances and take up collections for the poor.

Sometime during those two days, congregations will meet at their synagogues and eat a big meal called "Esther's Feast." Then they will all sit down to hear the book of Esther read in its entirety. The book of Esther must be read from a hand-written scroll called a [Megillah]{.class_3429}. Whenever the name of [Haman ]{.class_3429}is read, members of the congregation will stomp their feet, bang mallets on the wooden pew, twirl noisemakers, and hiss.

That is where Americans get the habit of hissing the villain. The "original" is found in a King James Bible. Job 27:23 says, ["Men shall clap their hands at him, and shall hiss him out of his place."]{.class_3428} Job 23 is a chapter describing the Antichrist (see comments in the [Bible Believer's Commentary on Job]{.class_3429}, Bible Baptist Bookstore). And as we have already noted, Haman is one of the greatest types of the Antichrist.

Verses 24--25 are a synopsis of the plot of Esther.

["The book"]{.class_3428} of verse 32 is defined in Esther 10:2. It is ["the book of the chronicles of the kings of Media and Persia." ]{.class_3428}But as it turns out, ["the book" ]{.class_3428}also turns out to be the book of Esther. And although the word [God]{.class_3429} never occurs in the book, and although []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3169.xhtml_page_413}the writer never claims inspiration, the Lord has the book written and made a part of the Scriptures.

Job lamented,[ "Oh that my words were now written! Oh that they were printed in a book!" ]{.class_3428}(Job 19:23). And, ["Behold, my desire is, that the Almighty would answer me, and that mine adversary had written a book" ]{.class_3428}(Job 31:35). He did!

The Lord not only recorded the trouble of the Jews in Job, He also recorded [their triumph]{.class_3429} in Esther. [He put them both in a Book. ]{.class_3429}You can purchase a copy for as little as five dollars in some stores.

It lies on the shelves of billions throughout the world. It is a testimony of God's goodness to those will believe what it says, and it stands as a warning to all those who think that they are smarter than God Almighty. You will either break your fool neck by trying to [subvert ]{.class_3429}it, like Haman did, or you will [believe ]{.class_3429}it, claim it, and live by it like Mordecai and Esther.

["Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction. I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast quickened me. I am thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts. The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I will consider thy testimonies" ]{.class_3428}(Psa. 119:92--95).

[]{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3267.xhtml}

## Chapter 10 {.heading_98-0}

10:1 And the king Ahasuerus laid a tribute upon the land, and upon the isles of the sea.

2 And all the acts of his power and of his might, and the declaration of the greatness of Mordecai, whereunto the king advanced him, are they not written in the book of the chronicles of the kings of Media and Persia?

3 For Mordecai the Jew was next unto king Ahasuerus, and great among the Jews, and accepted of the multitude of his brethren, seeking the wealth of his people, and speaking peace to all his seed.

Esther 10 is God's "happily ever after" chapter to the book of Esther. That is the way a story should end. All of God's stories have happy endings for God's people. A story ought to end right, and if there is any God at all, [that is the way everything will end up.]{.class_3429}

You are living in a day when stories don't [end ]{.class_3429}right. These modern authors don't know how to [end ]{.class_3429}them right. One of the first writers to do that was Stephen Crane in [The Red Badge of Courage]{.class_3429}. It is an excellent work, and it gives a very accurate view of a man's emotions in combat. But stories like that don't end with any kind of [finality]{.class_3429}. They leave you hanging, wondering how the story [really ]{.class_3429}ends.

From that came a whole genre of that type of story. [Gone with the Wind]{.class_3429} is a good example. Rhett Butler is leaving Scarlet and saying, "Frankly, my dear, I don't give a d\_\_\_." And as the story closes all you know is that Scarlet plans on going back to Terra and starting life over again.

Well? Does she make it? Do Rhett and Scarlet get back together again? Or does she make another mess of things and die a lonely, bitter, forsaken woman? Who knows? [Who cares?]{.class_3429}

These novels by Ernest Hemmingway and James Joyce and William Faulkner have no [end ]{.class_3429}because the unsaved guys writing them are trying to be realistic. If you are realistic (and lost), [there are no solutions.]{.class_3429}

James Jones wrote a book titled [From Here to Eternity]{.class_3429}. It is an []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3267.xhtml_page_415}amazing book. Of course it's a dirty book; it's full of filth; but it's real. [It is real because people are full of filth.]{.class_3429}

That book ends with a woman throwing a lei over the back end of a boat to see if it will sink behind the boat. The Japanese have just bombed Pearl Harbor, and she is leaving Hawaii with her little eleven-year-old boy. The boy is talking about joining the army because his dad is in the military and is about to be shipped out to the war in the Pacific. She tells her son that he is too young to get in that war. So the little boy asks, "Mom, do you think I can get in the [next one?"]{.class_3429} She says, ["Maybe."]{.class_3429}

Period. That's the [end ]{.class_3429}of the book.

Don't you worry. [He got in the next one. ]{.class_3429}He got into the Korean War.

These modern stories [end that way]{.class_3429} because all an [unsaved man]{.class_3429} can give you is a stream of consciousness. He's existential. He can only give what is taking place at the moment. [Nothing is settled because there aren't any answers in the present moment.]{.class_3429}

Music has gotten like that. When a classical composer ended a piece, you [knew]{.class_3429} that it was ended. That [coda ]{.class_3429}went on so long that when it was over, IT WAS OVER. In this modern generation, the rock singer doesn't know how to [end ]{.class_3429}a song so the soundboard technician electronically fades the music out, and the thing trails off. Why? [Because they don't know how to end a piece.]{.class_3429}

That's a picture of an unsaved man who doesn't know where he is going or how to get there. [He doesn't know from he came, he doesn't know what he is doing here, and he doesn't know where he is going. ]{.class_3429}He's like Mohammed.

God's books aren't like that. [They end right.]{.class_3429}

The old fairy stories (I mean real fairies; not this bunch of modern sex perverts) are like that. They aren't Bible stories, but they[ end right. ]{.class_3429}They have a [happy ending]{.class_3429}. Usually those stories end with the hero and the heroine going off together to live together and a wicked witch getting what's coming to her.

I like stories like that. I especially like to read about the wicked witch[ burning to death. ]{.class_3429}It's so Biblical.

If you think me rather twisted and peculiar for taking that view, you need to read your Bible. At the end of the book of Revelation, a []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3267.xhtml_page_416}"woman" burns. When she does, the people up in Heaven are shouting, "Hallelujah, let 'er burn!" (Rev. 18--19) So I am not quite as odd as you think I am.

As the book of Esther comes to a close, the king is reigning over the entire civilized world, and men are bringing him their tribute.

The last time we saw Esther was in Esther 9:32. But her story ends with her in complete favor with the king (Esth. 9:12) and exercising ["all authority"]{.class_3428} (Esth. 9:29).

Mordecai has been ["advanced"]{.class_3428} to ["greatness" ]{.class_3428}(vs. 2) by the king. He's ["next unto king Ahasuerus." ]{.class_3428}He's ["great among the Jews." ]{.class_3428}He's ["accepted of the multitude of his brethren." ]{.class_3428}He's ["seeking the wealth of his people."]{.class_3428} He's ["speaking peace to all his seed."]{.class_3428}

Did you notice how much of what was said about Mordecai reminds you of Joseph back in Genesis? The book of Genesis ends with Joseph second in power to Pharaoh and with all his brothers bowing down to him (Gen. 50:18). He's finally been accepted by a bunch of siblings who hated his guts back in Genesis 37. At the [end ]{.class_3429}he takes cares of his brothers and their families and raises his children and grandchildren and great grandchildren in peace (Gen. 50:21--23).

Joseph is a type of Christ in 153 particulars.

So what you have in Esther 10 is a picture of how the Bible [ends;]{.class_3429} especially in regards to Jesus Christ and the Jews. In Revelation 21 and 22, God Almighty is on the throne of the universe (Rev. 22:3). The Lord Jesus Christ is reigning with His Father in the second position in the Trinity (Rev. 21:22--23, 22:1--3). The Gentiles are bringing the Lord their tribute (Rev. 21:24--26). Christ's greatness is recorded in a Book (Rev. 22:10--19). The Jews have finally accepted Him as their Messiah, and they have been given the world and all of its wealth (see comments on Rom. 4:13 in that commentary). And to those of us who are ["his seed," ]{.class_3428}He has given perfect, [everlasting peace ]{.class_3429}(Rev. 21:4).

Now, that is how it ought to [end]{.class_3429}. You can't imagine God, if He can do anything and everything, working out things so that[ in the end]{.class_3429} everyone continues to suffer, everyone continues to weep, or everything ends in eternal darkness and annihilation. If there is any []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3267.xhtml_page_417}God up there, He has to be perfect. If He is perfect, He has to be holy. [Holiness ]{.class_3429}implies righteousness. So if there is a God, He has to find some way to punish unrighteousness and reward righteousness, or He's not there.

That reasoning is what creates [atheists]{.class_3429}. A man looks around and sees some bad fellow who seems to be just fine. He's done wrong and gotten away with it. Then the guy sees a man who lives right and is going through all kinds of trouble that the bad fellow isn't experiencing at all. He sees that inequity and figures there's no God.

But that won't do. That atheist didn't figure on eternity. Life doesn't end [down here]{.class_3429}. If God doesn't punish or reward a man [down here]{.class_3429}, He will in eternity.

Just as sure as you are reading this page, there are people out in the world who have committed horrible crimes. They have never been caught, and they haven't been punished.

People say that there is no such thing as a perfect crime. [Sure there is. ]{.class_3429}Who was convicted of the murders of "Jack the Ripper"? Nobody! Who went to prison for the Green River murders? Nobody! Did anybody get the "hot squat" for the Zodiac killings? No!

Brethren, there are a lot of bodies that have never been found. [There are a lot of murders that will never be solved.]{.class_3429}

I would like to see you convict and imprison [anybody ]{.class_3429}for the murder of Jimmy Hoffa. Nobody has found the body yet. For all intents and purposes whoever did it "got away with murder."

At the same time, there are people who have done all kinds of good deeds and have never been paid back for doing them. There are people who are self-sacrificing, and they take care of others. They may be poor or sickly because of their self-denial and die ten years before their time. [They received no reward down here.]{.class_3429}

What was Stephen's reward for preaching the truth? He got "rocked" to sleep! John the Baptist was beheaded for trying to get a king to do right. John Huss was burned at the stake because he trusted a bunch of Catholics to keep their word.

Beloved, if there is any God up there, [one day He is going to settle accounts.]{.class_3429}

Now, if you are saved, you have Christ's righteousness. One day the Lord is going to reward that righteousness: [He is going to []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3267.xhtml_page_418}reward you someday.]{.class_3429}

Some day there will be no more pain, no more sorrow, no more bills, no more taxes, no more family troubles, no more trouble with your kids, no more balding head, no more loose teeth, no more aches, no more arthritis, no more leukemia, no more diabetes, no more falling chest, no more falling arches, no more bladder trouble, no more kidney stones, no more gall stones, no more ulcers, no more trouble with your colon, no more upset stomach, no more acid "reflux," no broken bones, no broken heart, no coffin, no doctor bills, no ambulances, no hospitals---[everything's right!]{.class_3429}

I don't know about you, but I'm ready to go today! The quicker the better.

"Even so, come, Lord Jesus!"

## Appendix I {.heading_98-1}

"Keeping Up With The Times"

(A word on Chronology)

When we get into the ["times of the Gentiles,"]{.class_3428} we move in on Nebuchadnezzar in 606 B.C., for he is the king who is going to finish off Israel by taking Judah into captivity after Sennacherib and Shalmanesser finish off the ten northern tribes (2 Kings 17). [Benjamin,]{.class_3429} of course, is "inclusive" with Judah (see 1 Kings 11:13) due to the bond established centuries ago (Gen. 44) between the two brothers, long before Israel became a nation.

Now, when anyone---the best of 'em---gets fooling with [dates]{.class_3429} they run into trouble. Gregory, Clinton, Ptolemy, Ussher, Thucydides, Sir Robert Anderson, Scofield, Larkin, Bullinger, and Newton "have a time of it" keeping up with "the times."

I have read books on Biblical chronology to prove that Adam was created on the sabbath, that Noah got into the ark on the sabbath (and came out on the sabbath), that Isaac was taken up to Mt. Moriah to be sacrificed on the sabbath, and that Joseph got out of jail on the sabbath. Obviously the chronologist was a Seventy-day Adventist; what else?

Bullinger has, in the back of his [Companion Bible,]{.class_3429} 198 "Appendices" which you must admit are a pretty good bit of "ad libbing" after finishing 1,914 pages of "text." Appendices 57--58 deal with the [Persian kings]{.class_3429} in the times of Ezra and Nehemiah. They are preceded by Appendix No. 50, which proports to give you the Biblical material dealing with forty centuries (Adam to Christ) [one year at a time,]{.class_3429} year by year. You would think that such a detailed work could not possibly be in error, but Bullinger, more than any other chronologist, gets so screwed up that he winds up with the destruction of the temple by "Nebby" taking place in 497 B.C., which is about 100 years "off base" with Ussher, Rimmer, Newton, and others.

Bullinger has Malachi's epistle written in 374 B.C. Ussher and others would place it at 397. How Bullinger caught up seventy-seven []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3312.xhtml_page_420}of the years he dropped I don't know. He was one hundred years ahead in Zedekiah's time, but somewhere between Zedekiah (2 Kings 25) and Malachi he picked up seventy-seven years; that is, he came back up to within twenty-three years of Ussher's chronology during the Ezra-Nehemiah period.

Bullinger got into this "timely" madhouse by fooling with ["the fourth year of Jehoiakim"]{.class_3428} (Appendix 86). This runs into five pages of very small print. Here Bullinger deals with Newton's chronology, Ptolemy's chronology, Censorinus' chronology, Ussher's chronology, Clinton's chronology, and some others.

The crux of the matter is that Bullinger [rejects]{.class_3429} what he calls "the traditional" date of the first Greek Olympiad, which was recorded in 776 B.C. He offers, for this, his own system of dating beginning with Adam and then marking every year [one year at a time]{.class_3429} to Jehoiakim. This can overlook, of course, some things that no one could afford to overlook: [consecutive reigns]{.class_3429} of kings with gaps between them (1 and 2 Kings), [dual reigns]{.class_3429} of two kings at one time (1 and 2 Kings and 1 and 2 Chronicles), [overlaps]{.class_3429} of events (Judges) where the liberating judges are not "consecutive," and so forth. You can think you have every year accounted for when you don't, and you can think a year needs to be inserted where it [overlapped]{.class_3429} a period of years. Bullinger had good intentions, but then when he hits Ezra and Nehemiah, the berry basket caves in.

The "twenty years of Artaxerxes" finishes him off (see the comments under that verse (Neh. 1:1). In Nehemiah 1:1, he cannot even locate [the beginning]{.class_3429} of the "twentieth year." It has been located by an [anonymous chronologist]{.class_3429} who has produced the finest, most accurate, most Biblical chronology I have ever studied. This absolutely unknown Bible believer is a "dark horse" named "Floyd Jones"---how is that for anonymity!? His work---a fifty-foot chart listing every year since 4000 B.C. ([exactly like Bullinger had done]{.class_3429})---justifies [every year]{.class_3429} and date given in a [King James Bible.]{.class_3429}

All I see on my five scrolls (literal "rolls"---each one running ten feet) is "Floyd Jones Ministries Inc." ([Chronology of the Old Testament, ]{.class_3429}Floyd Jones, is available from Bible Baptist Bookstore \[includes CD of the charts\]).

But "one of the Jones boys" (American, "Wimpy" in Popeye, []{#I1HHcIZkQh_UMLBZXzVcAA3312.xhtml_page_421}circa 1930--1940) straightened Bullinger, Scofield, Sir Robert Anderson, Thucydides, and Clinton out like unrolling a roll of barbed wire.

Without going into a long thing, I am giving the dates as Floyd Jones would give them in the Zedekiah--Nehemiah period (588--445 B.C.). The only change I made was to [begin]{.class_3429} the date of the seventy years captivity at 589 B.C.---the final destruction of Jerusalem---instead of 598 (the capture of ["Jehoiachin"]{.class_3428}). Jones has "Nebby" attacking Jerusalem [three times]{.class_3429} (602, 598, and 589 B.C.).

So 589, minus 70, would end the captivity in 519 B.C. During that time Babylon would be overthrown (538 B.C.), and Media-Persia would take over. Following the [King James ]{.class_3429}text, Jones puts DARIUS and CYRUS on the throne in 538 B.C. One was king of "Media" (["Darius the Median,"]{.class_3428} Dan. 5:31); the other was CYRUS, king over Persia.This [dual kingdom]{.class_3429} lasts two years, so Cyrus is the sole ruler from 536 to 529 B.C. This is the ["Cyrus"]{.class_3428} who issued the decree in 2 Chronicles 36 and Ezra 1.

The ["first year"]{.class_3428} of his reign over an unified kingdom (not "Media-Persia:) would be 536 B.C. This matches all accounts.

Jones agrees with Bullinger on the matter of such names as ["Darius," "Xerxes,"]{.class_3428} and ["Artaxerxes"]{.class_3428} being "appelatives" (titles, like Pharaoh, Caesar, et al.). Jones gives THREE "Dariuses": "Darius" (538--529 B.C.), Darius Hystaspis (521--486 B.C.), and Darius I (521----485 B.C.). The last "Darius" has a co-reign with Artaxerxes (Xerxes I) in 505 B.C., and Artaxerxes (Xerxes) reigns [soley]{.class_3429} from 485--465 B.C., at which time Artaxerxes (Longimanus) takes over till 424 B.C. A fourth "Darius" shows up between 423--404 B.C.

This system will make the twentieth year of one Artaxerxes (Neh. 1:1: Xerxes) an exact twenty years from 505 B.C. when he began a joint reign with Darius (Ezra 6).

Now, all of these "sheenanigans" are efforts to line up the Bible with secular historical recordings, and this is always a "rough trip." For the God of the Bible is the God of history, while the ["god of this WORLD"]{.class_3428} is dedicated to ridding this world of the Bible. This means that he will give you one set of "historical facts" to match [his own "reign" as a god]{.class_3429} (2 Cor. 4:4) while the Bible will give you the true, [historical facts]{.class_3429} tht match [God's reign]{.class_3429} (as in Dan. 2,7,9).

So here is Bullinger, laid alongside Jones, with Jones' material matching the dates in the [AV Holy Bible]{.class_3429} and Bullinger's messing them up. The first column is [Joneses',]{.class_3429} the second one is [Bullinger's:]{.class_3429}

[Cyrus and Darius together]{.class_3438}[​]{.class_3462}[Cyrus I]{.class_3438}

Cyrus' decree 536 B.C.

[Cambyses]{.class_3438}[​]{.class_3460}[Cambyses]{.class_3438}

[Darius co-reign with Xerxes]{.class_3438}[​]{.class_3463}[Cyrus II]{.class_3438}

[Xerxes sole reign]{.class_3438}[​]{.class_3461}[Hystaspes]{.class_3438}

[Xerxes co-reign Artaxerxes Longimanus]{.class_3438}[​]{.class_3439}[Darius Hystaspes]{.class_3438}

Xerxes II

Darius II

You can see, at a glance, that chronologists "have a time of it."

Floyd Jones has confined himself to the Biblical text to get the historical dates; Bullinger, on the other hand, went first to Herodotus, the unsaved historian, then the Behistun Rock, and then the "Cylinder of Cyrus."

"When in doubt, throw "scholarship" out: O-U-T, OUT!!"
